           <a href="https://blossomthemes.com/wordpress-themes/blossom-studio-pro/" rel="bookmark">
            Blossom Studio Pro
           </a>
          </h3>
          <div class="entry-excerpt" itemprop="description">
           <p>
            Blossom Studio Pro is a lead generating WordPress theme to launch your yoga, dance, meditation or any studio into the digital world. This is a multi-purpose theme that can help you showcase your studio for yoga, meditation, dance, wellness retreat, and much more. This feature-rich theme has an elegant, photo-first design that creates the right atmosphere for your studio website.
           </p>
           <p>
            Blossom Studio Pro also comes with tailor-built inner page templates to support every aspect of your business. You get a pre-built landing page template to promote your programs, books, and products. You can showcase your courses through the Course page template, and there is even a Consultation page template to boost appointments and attract new customers.
           </p>

         <header class="entry-header" itemscope="">
          <h3 class="entry-title" itemprop="name">
           <a href="https://blossomthemes.com/wordpress-themes/travel-nomad/" rel="bookmark">
            Travel Nomad
           </a>
          </h3>
          <div class="average-rating download-aside">
           <strong>
            5.0
           </strong>
           <div class="edd_reviews_aggregate_rating_display">
            <div aria-label="5.00 stars" class="edd_reviews_rating_box" role="img">
             <div class="edd_star_rating" style="width: 95px">
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <p class="average-rating-count">
            <a href="https://blossomthemes.com/wordpress-themes/travel-nomad/#edd-reviews">
             (1 review)
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="entry-excerpt" itemprop="description">
           <p>
            Travel Nomad is an elegant free WordPress theme ideal to create sleek and feminine travel blogs. This responsive, SEO integrated, and speed optimized theme caters to all sorts of travel bloggers willing to share their experiences with the world.
           </p>
           <p>
            This theme comes with several predefined homepage sections to choose from. The built-in live customizer provides you control over the visual appeal of your site. You can change the color typography and fonts of your site to match your brand style.
           </p>
           <p>
            With Woocommerce’s support, you can easily create an online store and sell your merchandise. It also supports HTML 5 Maps, so marking the places you have visited is effortless.
           </p>
          </div>

             <b>
              Honestly the best theme in the world
             </b>
             <span class="edd-review-meta-rating">
              <span class="dashicons dashicons-star-filled">

              <span class="dashicons dashicons-star-filled">

            <div class="edd-review-metadata">
             <p>
              <span class="author">
               By 																													Nadiya Khan
              </span>
              on
              <time>
               May 22, 2019 at 9:35 pm
              </time>
              <span class="edd-reviews-verified-purchase">
               Verified Purchase
              </span>
             </p>

            <!-- .comment-metadata -->
           </div>
           <!-- .comment-meta -->
           <div class="edd-review-content">
            <p>
             I have been a WordPress user for over 5 years now. I have struggled so much with themes as none of the themes I ever used had a customer service which would actually respond. I had unlimited issues which never got resolved and I had to eventually keep changing my themes which required constant work.
            </p>
            <p>
             I thank my lucky stars for coming across Blossom Pro Themes last year. I started off with their free theme and then moved on to their Pro theme which is even more brilliant.
            </p>
            <p>
             The customer service is the best best part. They are literally one email away and fix every single issue you may have. The pro-theme has great customization options and accommodates most of the changes you may want. Anything that’s left is catered by their super-efficient support team.
            </p>
            <p>
             After years of changing themes for one reason or another, I have finally found a theme that I’m really content with. I can’t wait to change my mom and my sister’s website to this theme too as it’s super amazing.
            </p>
            <p>
             I HIGHLY HIGHLY recommend this theme as its modern, elegant and so professional.
            </p>
           </div>

             I purchased the Sarada theme after reading several recommendations about other Blossom Themes relating to page speed and mobile optimization. While exploring the Pro themes on the site, I noticed the Sarada release. I reviewed the extensive information provided and tested the demo. This theme has not disappointed. It took a few minutes to install. There is full documentation provided with all questions answered on how to set up and customize your site. I have had several questions during my setup process relating to my own personal requirements for my blog and website, and I have had the best experience with the Blossom Themes team, especially Nabin. Every question I have asked has been resolved, with detailed responses and information provided. The team have gone above and beyond to ensure that my site can do what I need it to do. My site has also had a noticeable increase in traffic since I began using this theme, and my performance speed has increased. I am so impressed and I am very happy that I purchased the Sarada Pro theme. I highly recommend it for any blogger. Thank you so much!
